1.0 Initial Draft  11/28/2006  Partner Cert 
Team Initial Creation of Document 
1.3 Draft  03/27/2007  Partner Cert 
Team The following message structures 
have been modified slightly to 
incorporate RCL specific extensions. 
• OTA_CruiseSailAvailRQ 
• OTA_CruiseSailAvailRS 
• OTA_CruiseBookRQ 
• OTA_CruisePricingRS 
• RCL_LoginRQ 
• RCL_LoginRS 
In addition to this, minor changes have 
been made to 
OTA_CruiseCommonTypes to 
accommodate RCL specific 
extensions. 
1.4 Draft 05/16/2007  Partner Cert 
Team  • Included the below messages in 
the document. 
• Cruise Package Detail 
• Cruise Validate Linked 
Bookings 
• Cruise Payment Extension 
• Cruise Option Detail 
• Changed format of typical process 
flows to be UML based for better 
readability 
• Updated schema text with changes  
• Changed references from 
Availability to List in all messages 
since the messages also return 
unavailable entries with a status 
indicating no availability. 
• Added message specific and 
global extensions and restrictions. 
• Updated reusable data types for 
each message 
• Changed some of the message 
names to be more indicative of the  
actual underlying operations. 
 
1.5 Draft 06/15/2007  Partner Cert 
Team • Changes for the 2007A release of 
the schema files incorporated into 
the specification. 
1.6 Draft 09/14/2007  Partner Cert 
Team • Updated sample API messages  
that are schema valid.

in Option List response 
parameters.

Page 16 of 382 1. General 
1.1 Purpose 
This Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd. (RCL) Cruise API  specification describes the basic 
transactions that are required to shop for, create,  and make changes to an RCL booking. 
These RCL API specifications apply to the RCI, Cele brity and Island cruises brands. 
 
It will also describe the necessary processes to re trieve a booking for amendments or to 
make payments along with additional transactions th at are used to select and book certain 
enhanced services such as bus transfers, tours and special services. Additional details 
include the connectivity sections and will also add ress administrative issues such as 
testing criteria and change control. 
 
The purpose of the document is to describe the avai lable messages for use and to provide 
guidelines on “HOW TO” connect with and use all the  information and functionality that 
this API provides. The goals of this document are t o: 
 
• Describe the purpose and processing services of eac h message 
• Describe each  transaction’s request/response XML s chemas 
• Document an example of a navigation path that will be supported 
• Provide the technical requirements for connecting t o the RCL Cruise API 
• Provide the standards for full system testing 
Note:  This version of the specification includes o perations for Full Individual Tariff 
(FIT) only. The API specification for Groups functi onality is made available as part of a 
separate document. 
1.2 Disclaimers 
This RCL Cruise API specification includes content derived from the OpenTravel™ 
Alliance (OTA) 2007A specification and is subject t o the terms as set forth in the OTA 
License Agreement. 
 
Please review and agree to the OTA license agreemen t and download the OTA 2007A 
specification here:  http://opentravel.org/2007A.cfm  
1.3 API Connectivity 
Connectivity to the RCL Cruise API will use SOAP ov er HTTPS over the public Internet 
to send and receive partner messages.  Uniform Reso urce Locators (URL)s required to 
access the API and the required Web Service Descrip tion Language (WSDL) files are 
bundled with this specification document.  Also, RC L requires partners to send, with 
every web service request, HTTP Basic Authenticatio n credentials issued by the RCL 
Certification team. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

The RCL Cruise API network configuration is as foll ows:

DISASTER RECOVERY https://dr .services.rccl.com 12.172.40.29

access test environment with the following configur ation:

This information will prove useful for partners to preconfigure their network 
infrastructure to access RCL services over the Inte rnet. 
 
1.4 System Testing 
The RCL test environment resides within separate in frastructure than the one used for the 
live production environment.  Test data will be see ded with an extract of production data 
and may not be a true representation or exact copy of production scenarios. Due to the 
changing nature of test inputs, the validity of tes t scenarios will be the responsibility of 
the testers involved. 
1.5 FIT Message List 
Message Name Message Description 
Cruise Login This transaction is used to authenticate the Agent that 
has logged on and will return the required agency 
information to be populated in the POS header for a ll 
subsequent transactions.  In the case of Global 
Distribution Systems, this message is not required but 
useful since it provides RCL specific information s uch 
as agency restrictions, valid payment methods, 
currencies, and insurance information.  
Cruise Agency Lookup  This transaction is used to authenticate and lookup  the 
Agent that has logged on and will return the requir ed 
agency information to be populated in the POS heade r 
for all subsequent transactions.  In the case of Gl obal 
Distribution Systems, this message is not required but 
useful since it provides RCL specific information s uch 
as agency restrictions, valid payment methods, 
currencies, and insurance information. 
Cruise Sailing List The Sailing List Request message requests a listing  of Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 18 of 382 available and unavailable sailings for a date range , for a 
specific geographic region and/or a specific ship c ode.  
Additional filters are available for embarkation po rt, 
dining seating, and brand. 
The response message returns a list of sailings mat ching 
the specified criteria.  
Cruise Package List The Cruise Package List message is used to request 
information about the CruiseTour packages associate d 
with a sailing.   
Cruise Dining List The Cruise Dining List message is used to determine  
what dinign seating options are available for a giv en 
sailing.  Dining seating types include Traditional ( i.e. 
Main and Second), Open Dining, and Undecided. 
Cruise Transfer List The Cruise Transfer List message is used to request  
information about the transfers associated with a s ailing. 
Transfers allow guests to obtain transportation fro m the 
airport to the ship and vice versa. The response me ssage 
contains a list of transfers along with the associa ted 
pricing for them.   
Cruise Bus List The Cruise Bus List message is used to request 
information about the buses that transport passenge rs 
from predetermined stops to the ship.  
The response message contains a list of buses that pick 
up passengers at pre-determined locations and trans port 
them to the ship. 
Cruise Tour List The Cruise Tour List message is used to request 
information such as the duration and description of  a 
cruise package.  
The response message contains a list of tour packag es 
along with the associated details such as duration and 
pricing for these tour packages.  
Cruise Bus Detail The Cruise Bus Detail message is used to request 
detailed information about the buses that transport  the 
passengers from predetermined stops to the ship.   
The response message contains the details of the 
requested buses along with the associated location and 
start times. 
Cruise Package Detail The Cruise Package Detail message is used to reques t 
detailed information about the pre-cruise, post-cru ise, or 
the inclusive-cruise packages associated with a sai ling.  
A cruise package can be a stay in a hotel for one o r more 
days at the beginning or end of a cruise, cruise on ly 
transfers between the ship and the airport, or buse s that 
transport the passengers from predetermined stops t o the 
ship.  In the case of a hotel, it is generally loca ted near 
the port of embarkation or debarkation.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 19 of 382  
The response message contains the details of the 
requested package along with the associated pricing  for 
the package.  
Cruise Tour Detail The Cruise Tour Detail message is used to request 
detailed textual information about the tour. 
 
The response message contains the details of the 
requested tours along with the associated pricing f or 
these tours, hotel addresses etc. 
Cruise Transfer Detail The Cruise Package Detail message is used to reques t 
detailed information about the pre-cruise, post-cru ise, or 
the inclusive-cruise packages associated with a sai ling.  
A cruise package can be a stay in a hotel for one o r more 
days at the beginning or end of a cruise, cruise on ly 
transfers between the ship and the airport, or buse s that 
transport the passengers from predetermined stops t o the 
ship.  In the case of a hotel, it is generally loca ted near 
the port of embarkation or debarkation.  
 
The response message contains the details of the 
requested packages along with the associated pricin g for 
these packages. 
Cruise Category List The Category List Request message requests a list o f 
cabin rate categories for a specified sailing and f are 
code. The sailing information is indicated by the s hip 
and departure date. 
The response message returns a list of cabin rate 
categories that correspond to the requested sailing  and 
fare.  
Cruise Category List Version 
2.0 The new version supports category/pricing informati on 
for upto two different rate concepts. 
The response message returns a list of cabin rate 
categories that corresponds to the requested sailin g and 
Fare codes(s). The new response structure is in a m ore 
readable format. 
Cruise Cabin List The Cabin List Request message requests a list of 
available cabins for a selected category on a saili ng. The 
sailing information is defined by the departure dat e and 
ship. The fare code and the berthed and priced cate gory 
codes are retained from the respective list message . 
 
The response message returns a list of cabins match ing 
the specified criteria.  
Cruise Cabin Detail The Cabin Detail Request message requests details o f a Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 20 of 382 selected cabin for a selected category on a sailing .  
 
The response message returns a list of cabin attrib utes 
such as size for the requested cabin. 
Cruise Cabin Hold The Cruise Cabin Hold request message instructs RCL  
to put a temporary hold on selected cabin(s) for a short 
time interval (interval is currently set at fifteen  minutes) .  
This allows the user time to enter additional 
information, which is required to complete the book ing 
without concern for losing the cabin.  The sailing is 
identified by the ship and departure date.  RCL cur rently 
allows up to four cabins to be held at a time. 
The response message indicates the status of each c abin 
for which a hold is requested.  
Cruise Cabin Release The Cruise Cabin Release request message is used to  
release a hold that was previously placed on a cabi n and 
to release the cabin into the available inventory. 
The response message indicates the status for the c abin 
in the request.   
Cruise Fare List This transaction returns a list of the promotional 
programs that are applicable to a selected ship, sa il date, 
and other guest requirements. 
 
The Fare List Request message requests a listing of  
available fares for a selected RCL sailing.  The sh ip and 
departure date identifies the sailing. The guest co unt 
structure is used to communicate the number of gues ts 
that will be sailing.  Although Guest Transportatio n 
information is optional, in normal practice it is a dvisable 
to enter the mode of transportation and gateway cit y 
because some fares have restrictions based on 
transportation. 
The response message returns a list of all Base 
fares/Promotional Fares, including agency specific 
restricted fares, for which the traveler qualifies based 
upon the criteria provided.  
Cruise Fare Detail This transaction returns the details pertaining to a 
selected fare such as the restrictions associated w ith the 
fare.  
The response message returns a list of fare details , 
including agency specific restricted fares, for whi ch the 
traveler qualifies based upon the criteria provided . 
Cruise Booking Price The Cruise Booking Price request message requests t he 
pricing for all components of a booking.  All of th e 
components to be purchased must be included in the Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 21 of 382 Cruise  Booking Price request. This includes the sa iling 
by using either the booking id or the ship and sail  date, 
the priced and berthed category, the fare code, the  
gateway, the pre and/or post land packages, and 
insurance. 
Asis  booking price can also be requested without 
constructing the entire request payload. 
The response message returns the pricing breakdown by 
component for both the booking and each guest.  
Cruise Validate Linked 
Bookings The Validate Linked Bookings Request message is use d 
to validate the cross reference booking numbers for  all 
the categories – Tours, Dining, and Air.  
Cruise Payment Extension The Cruise Payment Extension request message reques ts 
for an extension of the booking option date. Prior to 
invoking the payment extension message, the current  
option date may be retrieved through the booking 
retrieve or in the pricing request.  
Cruise Confirm Booking The Cruise Confirm Booking message is used to creat e a 
booking, amend a booking or cancel a booking on the  
RCL reservation system for a specific sailing, with  a 
specified mode of transportation/gateway city pair and 
currency, and a selected fare/category pair, for on e or 
more passengers in a specific cabin.  A payment can  be 
applied with this request. 
Prior to submitting a Confirm Booking request messa ge, 
a cabin must have been placed on hold.  The only 
exception to this is if a cabin is reserved as a gu arantee, 
rather than a specific cabin.  
Cruise Guest Option List The Cruise Guest Option List message is used to obt ain 
the list of guest options available on a given sail ing.   
Cruise Guest Services List The Cruise Guest Service List message is used to ob tain 
the list of guest services/options available on a g iven 
sailing. It can also be used to obtain details pert aining to 
a selected guest service.    
 
Cruise Option Detail The Cruise Option Detail message is used to obtain the 
detail of guest services/options available on a giv en 
sailing.  
Cruise Fast Sell The Cruise Fast Sell message requires the partner t o 
provide the mandatory ship and sail date informatio n. 
Optionally, category, price program, package code, and 
cabin information may be provided.  
Cruise Make Payment  The Cruise Make Payment message processes one 
credit card payment at a time and returns a confirm ation 
to the partner.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 22 of 382 Cruise Itinerary Detail The Cruise Itinerary Detail message is used to retu rn the 
itinerary details of the sailing.The message allows  travel 
customers to request the detailed itinerary for a s pecific 
sailing.The request message accepts a ship and sail  date 
to retrieve the itinerary.  
The response message contains the detailed itinerar y.   
Cruise Booking Document The Cruise Booking Document message provides the 
user the ability to request a document type and its  
delivery method without retrieving the reservation.   
 
Retrieve Booking The Retrieve Booking message uses the RCL booking 
ID to retrieve and assemble all the components of a  
booking, to include cruise, air details, and tour 
information. 
RCL intends to support booking retrieval by guest name.   
This will be included with the next specification r elease.  
Get Booking List The Get Booking List message is used to retrieve a list 
of bookings that are owned by the agency.  
The response message includes a list of bookings ow ned 
by the agency. 
Release Booking The Release Booking message uses the RCL booking ID  
to release the lock on the booking so that it can b e 
modified by another entity. 
Cruise Booking History This transaction uses the booking ID assigned by RC L 
to get the history of revisions and/or transformati ons 
related to that booking.  
The Cruise Booking History message requests 
change/service history on an existing reservation. The 
request message is the OTA_ReadRQ where the user 
can specify the Reservation ID for which one wishes  to 
see the change history. OTA_ReadRQ is also used to 
retrieve the reservation information. In order to 
distinguish the service history request from the re trieval 
of the reservation information a /g1oolean variable is 
used. The response message 
OTA_CruiseBookingHistoryRS returns a list of histor y 
entries for the reservation changes that have taken  place.  
PromoSearchBreakDown This transaction returns the Pricing break down for  a 
given Promotion/Lead Promotion. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 23 of 382 PromoDetailBreakDown This is similar to Fare Detail service in a new for mat. 
This transaction returns the details pertaining to a 
selected fare(s) such as the restrictions associate d with 
the fare.

1.7 Specification Schemas 
This version of the RCL Cruise API specification is  based on the OTA 2007A 
specification.  This specification document is acco mpanied by XSD schema files which 
extend the OTA 2007A specification. 
 
1.7.1 Overall Constraints and Restrictions 
The following two lists include constraints and res trictions for the overall RCL API 
implementation and have context across all applicab le API messages. 
1.7.1.1  Functional 
• Non cruise reservation information, such as air and  hotel, will always be 
dependent on the existence of a cruise reservation.  
• Guest element can repeat maximum of 4 times though schema allows 9 
occurrences. Additional occurrences are ignored in the implementation. 
• Guest Count element can repeat maximum of 4 times t hough schema allows 9 
occurrences. Additional occurrences are ignored in the implementation. Sum of 
quantity attribute specified in the GuestCount elem ent should not exceed 4. 
• Only 1 occurrence of SelectedCategory element with confirmed status must be 
provided inside SailingCategoryInfoType though sche ma supports 0 to 2 
occurrences. 2 nd  occurrence is ignored. The second occurrence will be supported 
in the case where the agent wishes to waitlist. 
• RCL requires a ship and a sail date to identify a s ailing uniquely and does not use 
Voyage ID. 
• RCL allows up to four cabins from a single sailing even though the schema allows 
cabins from up to three sailings to be held simulta neously. 
• RCL will only read currency information from the So urceType@ISOCurrency 
attribute in the POS header.  Any other document el ements by which currency 
information can be exchanged will be ignored. 
• Regarding the two occurrences of GuestTransportatio nType, only one should 
have confirmed status. The second occurrence will b e supported in the case where 
the agent wishes to waitlist. 
• A booking can have one confirmed cabin only. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 25 of 382 • All messages are checked for office and brand restr ictions prior to the message 
being processed. 
 
 
1.7.1.2  Non-Functional 
• Message payload should always use the ISO-8859-1 ch aracter set.  
• Date time format will conform with the XML schema s pecification (yyyy-MM-
ddThh:mm:ss) 
• Functional errors are populated inside the Warnings  element of the response

1.8.1 Use Cases

operation.  Please refer to the Functional Overview  and Transaction Services sections for 
further details. 
1.9 Error Handling 
Please refer error code appendix for a list of OTA error codes.   Note – At this time, OTA 
is yet to provide a numbering scheme for Cruise err or codes. 
1.10 Special Design Considerations 
1.10.1 Requirements 
• API clients are required to provide a unique Termin al ID 
(//POS/Source[1]/@TerminalID) across each client us er for every API call.  
Please refer to the Cruise API Header Specification  document for additional 
information. 
• It is the API client’s responsibility to generate s chema compliant messages and to 
log such messages in case of a message exchange fai lure. RCL infrastructure will 
reject invalid messages and does not log the payloa d of such messages in the 
production environment. 
1.10.2 Response Paging 
Some Cruise API messages provide the ability to pag e across resultsets.  Paging 
functionality is supported via the //<request schem a root>/@MaxResponses, //<request 
and response schema root>/@MoreDataEchoToken, and / /<response schema 
root>/@MoreIndicator.

2. Cruise Login Message 
2.1 Functional Overview 
This transaction is used to authenticate the Agent that has logged on and will return the 
required agency information to be populated in the POS header for all other transactions.  
In the case of Global Distribution Systems, this me ssage is not required but useful since it 
provides RCL specific information such as agency re strictions, valid payment methods, 
currencies, and insurance information. 
2.1.1 Transaction Services 
This request should be the first request for every session as it is required for the agency to 
be identified with each request.  If the partner ca n cache the POS header locally, this 
message request would not be mandatory.  The messag e response will include the agency 
phone number and details, default and alternate age ncy currencies, valid payment 
methods, overall agency restrictions for managing I ndividual and Group Reservations, 
insurance code, and brands. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 28 of 382

/ RCL_CruiseLoginRS

Page 35 of 382 3. Cruise Agency Lookup Message 
3.1 Functional Overview 
This message is very similar to the Cruise Login me ssage but is used to perform an 
agency lookup instead. This message is most useful when a headquarter/branch 
relationship exists between agencies.  
This transaction is used to authenticate the Agent that has logged on and will return the 
agency information requested based on a supplied ph one number. 
3.1.1 Transaction Services 
The agency lookup is allowed only if the requesting  agency is authorized to perform the 
lookup for the agency whose phone number is being s upplied in the request. 
 
3.2 Typical Process Flow 
 
 
 
 
3.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Agency Lookup request and response are RCL_CruiseLoginRQ and 
RCL_CruiseLoginRS.  Our implementation is not part of the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.  It is a Travel Partner extension. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

4. Cruise Sailing List Message 
4.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Sailing List Request message requests a listing  of available and unavailable sailings 
for a date range, for a specific geographic region and/or a specific ship code.  Additional 
filters are available for embarkation port and bran d. 
The response message returns a list of sailings mat ching the specified criteria.  RCL 
typically does not restrict the returned list of sa ilings to an exact request date, but will 
return sailings that fall within a time window arou nd the requested date. 
RCL identifies a sailing by a combination of ship a nd sailing date. 
The following optional search qualifiers are suppor ted for the Sailing List Message. 
• SailingDateRange 
o Start 
o End 
o Duration 
o Minimum duration 
o Maximum duration 
• CruiseLinePref 
o Vendor Code 
o Ship Code 
o Status 
o Port Code 
• Region Pref 
o Region Code 
Priced Category Code, Berthed Category Code, and Di ning are not supported by this 
message. 
4.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Defaults to all brands at RCL if no cruise line is provided. 
 
• Defaults Sailing Date to today’s date if no sailing  date is provided. 
 
• Provides sailings for up to 30 days past the select ed sailing start date or the 
current date. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 40 of 382  
• Defaults to all geographic regions if no geographic  area is provided. 
 
• Allows Selection by Region. 
 
• Every sailing returned in the response will indicat e the availability of a group 
reservation.  
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 41 of 382

The schemas for Cruise Sailing List request and res ponse are OTA_CruiseSailAvailRQ 
and OTA_CruiseSailAvailRS.  Our implementation is b ased on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.

Page 42 of 382 4.3.1.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information. 
• Searching by port under SearchQualifier is supporte d only if it is an originating 
port for a sailing. 
• Only one region/subregion for a sailing search even  though schema supports up to 
five. 
• Price search is not supported.

5. Cruise Package List Message 
5.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Package List message is used to request information about the inclusive-
cruise packages associated with a sailing and Cruis e Tours.  The response message 
contains a list of requested packages.   
 
When invoking this transaction, the PackageTypeCode  needs to be provided as per the 
OTA schema requirements but the value will not be p rocessed by RCL.  
 
In the response, the possible CruisePackageCodes ar e: 
• 1 – Cruise Tour 
• 2 – Expedition 
• 3 - Other 
5.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Allows for selection of packages from multiple depa rtures (using a date range in 
the request) or from only one departure. 
 
• If a package is included, it returns the package to urs with the actual package tour 
code.  
 
5.2 Typical Process Flow 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 47 of 382 
 
 
5.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Package List request and res ponse are OTA_CruisePkgAvailRQ 
and OTA_CruisePkgAvailRS.  Our implementation is ba sed on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.

Page 52 of 382 6. Cruise Dining List Message 
6.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Dining List message is used used to prov ide dining availability for RCL 
cruise inventory.   
 
Three dining seating types are to be initially conf igured by RCL.  These are to be used as 
part of the transactions where dining functionality  is implemented.  
o Traditional ( same as today) 
/square4 Main seating 
/square4 Second seating 
o Open 
o Undecided 
 
Additional dining seatings might be configured and partners will be notified via the 
normal change notification mechanisms. 
 
Dining limits can be configured for specific cruise  categories and loyalty levels.  
Therefore, the client application can optionally pr ovide those filters for the appropriate  
availability processing. 
 
At the time of writing, the Open dining seating typ e will require for gratuities to be pre-
paid. 
 
6.1.1 Transaction Services 
6.2 Typical Process Flow 
6.2.1 Create Mode 
Since dining availability is no longer supported as  part of the Sailing List and Category 
List messages, RCL recommends client applications t o send a Dining List message right 
after the user selects a Sailing or Category of int erest.  Please note that the guest dining 
preference is now required as part of the Price Boo king message. 
 
Error! Objects cannot be created from editing field  codes.  
 
6.2.2 Amend Mode 
 
RCL recommends that client applications send a Dini ng List messages right after 
Retrieve Booking and prior to Price Booking ( Amend ) so that the new dining rules be 
processed prior to repricing and amending the exist ing booking.  
 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 53 of 382 RCL Partner 
Booking Retrieval 
/OTA_ResRetrieveRS 
DiningList Booking Booking Id 
 
 
6.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Dining List request and resp onse are 
OTA_CruiseDiningAvailRQ and OTA_CruiseDiningAvailRS .  Our implementation is 
based on the OTA_2007A schema specification.

8. Cruise Bus List Message 
8.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Bus List message is used to request info rmation about the bus transportation 
between the ship and the airport, or buses that tra nsport the passengers from 
predetermined stops to the ship.  The response mess age contains a list of buses that 
provide transportation between the airport or other  pre-determined location and the cruise 
ship along with the associated pricing details.   
 
When calling the Bus List operation, the PackageTyp eCode should be set to the 
appropriate value from the OTA Code Table CPK. 
 
8.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Returns the available buses for the requested saili ng.  
 
• Indicates the availability status of a Bus, Bus Cha rge, Bus Stops etc. 
 
8.2 Typical Process Flow

9. Cruise Tour List Message 
9.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Tour List message is used to request inf ormation about the tours associated 
with a sailing. The response message includes detai ls pertaining to the tours such as the 
tour duration, description, availability, pricing a nd tour location codes.  
 
When calling the Tour List operation, the PackageTy peCode should be set to the 
appropriate value from the OTA Code Table CPK.  The  message currently supports the 
following PackageTypeCodes: 
 
10 – Pre cruise hotels 
11 – Post cruise hotels 
12 – Both Pre and Post hotels 
9.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• For tours (hotel stays) returns the available ones for each gateway.  
 
• For tours (hotel stays), provides the ability to in clude tours selected from another 
city besides the gateways. 
 
• For tours (hotel stays), indicates when it is requi red, free or optional.  
 
9.2 Typical Process Flow

10. Cruise Bus Detail Message

The Cruise Bus Detail message is used to request in formation about the bus legs along 
with the route timings for a particular bus.

11. Cruise Package Detail Message 
11.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Package Detail message is used to reques t detailed information about the pre-
cruise, post-cruise, or the inclusive-cruise packag es associated with a sailing.  The 
response message contains the details of the reques ted package along with the associated 
pricing for these packages.   
 
The package code should be provided in the request to retrieve the associated details. 
11.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Retrieves the detailed information pertaining to th e package for which the 
package code is provided. 
11.2 Typical Process Flow 
 
Partner RCCL 
Packages/Tours/Transfers/Buses Details Package/Tour/Transfer/Bus Detail 
/ OTA_ScreenTextRS / OTA_CruisePkgAvailRQ Packages List Package List / OTA_CruisePkgAvailRQ 
/ OTA_CruisePkgAvailRS

OTA_2007A schema specification.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

12. Cruise Tour Detail Message 
12.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Tour Detail message is very similar to t he Cruise Package Detail message and 
is  used to request detailed information about the hotel tours associated with a sailing.  A 
cruise package can be a stay in a hotel for one or more days at the beginning or end of a 
cruise.  They are generally located near the port o f embarkation or debarkation.  The 
response message contains the details of the reques ted tour packages along with theis 
associated pricing.  
 
The package code is mandatory as part of this reque st. 
12.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Retrieves the detailed information pertaining to th e tour package for which the 
package code is provided.

13. Cruise Transfer Detail Message 
13.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Transfer Detail message is very similar to the Cruise Package Detail message 
and is used to request detailed information about t he cruise transfers associated with a 
sailing. Cruise transfers are used to transport gue sts between the ship and the airport. 
The response message contains the details of the re quested transfers in textual free form. 
 
The package code should be provided in the request to retrieve the associated details. 
13.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Displays the detailed information of the cruise tra nsfer associated with the sailing.

14. Cruise Category List Message 
14.1 Functional Overview 
The Category List Request message requests a list o f cabin rate categories for a specified 
sailing and fare code. The sailing information is i ndicated by the ship and sail date. 
The response message returns a list of cabin rate c ategories that correspond to the 
requested sailing, fare code and Guest level promot ional qualifiers in addition to their 
respective status by occupancy, the category locati on on the ship, priced and berthed 
codes, as well as category pricing.  
14.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Validates the air status when gateway is provided 
 
• Validates the promo code for each category/occupanc y combination and returns 
the lowest available price for each combination 
 
• Returns a list of all cabin categories and 1/2/3/4 occupancy status and pricing 
information.  Returns a list of all cabin categorie s, status and pricing for the 
requested occupancy . Additionally, it includes 
- Location parameter – Inside, Outside, Balcony, and Deluxe 
- Promo code for best pricing for each category/occup ancy combination for 
available categories 
- Cruise only amounts 
- Air add-on amounts when gateways provided in the re quest 
 
• Returns FIT pricing when categories are not availab le. Prevailing base prices will 
be returned for Waitlisted categories.  
 
• The results are sent for all occupancy levels regar dless of the number specified in 
the request. The results are sent specific to the n umber of guests specified in the 
request. 
 
• The Lowest Available Fare ‘LAF’ concept is now bein g referred as ‘Best Rate’. 
 
• If the requested fare code is “LAF/BESTRATE”, then the response includes the 
Best rates for the given category/occupancy combina tion and the fare code used 
across all applicable fare codes.  
 
• If the requested fare code is “BVL” (Best Value), t hen the response includes any 
applicable best offer. If Best offer is not availab le, Best Rate will be returned with 
an info message. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 87 of 382 • The CategoryLocation attribute will not be returned  for virtual categories or 
categories used for guarantee cabins. 
 
• The response will include the highest configured ca tegory upgrade (berthed) for a 
given category (priced) when auto-upgrades are conf igured for a given category. 
 
• For sailings with a requirement for mandatory pre-p aid gratuities, an indicator 
(“A”) is sent back in the response to indicate grat uities are to be added to the 
booking and sent at confirmation time, unless the e nd customer has explicitly 
declined the gratuities later in the booking proces s.   
 
• For sailings with a requirement for Automated Manda tory pre-paid gratuities, an 
indicator (“M”) is send back in the response to ind icate gratuities will be added 
automatically to the booking at pricing and confirm ation time. These gratuities are 
not declinable in the booking process. 
 
• Accessible/Non-Accessible Stateroom qualifiers will  be accepted in the request. 
Category availability reponse will be returned base d on the accessible/non-
accessible staterooms availability. API partners ma y choose to opt out for the 
qualifier and continue getting the availability for  accessible and non-accessible 
staterooms. 
 
• Accessible Stateroom availability indicator will be  returned for every category in 
the response.  
 
• Connecting Stateroom qualifier will be accepted in the request. Response will 
return the availability based on the connecting sta teroom qualifier set in the 
request.  
 
• Connecting Stateroom availability indicator will be  returned for every category in 
the response. 
 
• Pricing and Promotions   
 
o The service request will accept optional promotion eligibility qualifiers at 
the guest level. Based on the promotional qualifier s the system will return 
the best rate (LAF/BESTRATE) along with any applica ble offers (BVL – 
Best Value). 
 
o If no promotional qualifiers are provided and BESTR ATE is requested, 
only unrestricted fares will be part of the calcula tion. 
 
o Request for a specific promotion will return a pric e based on the selected 
promotion, the corresponding best rate and any othe r unrestricted, 
combinable promotions. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 88 of 382 o Optional Guest level promotional qualifiers would i nclude 
Age/AgeQualifyingcode, Gateway code, Resident quali fiers 
(state/province), Occupational qualifiers (Military , Law enforcement, Fire 
Department, or EMT), coupon codes and Loyalty numbe rs. 
 
o Category Pricing for multiple combinable promotions  can also be 
requested. 
 
o Response is limited to occupancy requested. 
 
o FIT pricing concept is now being replaced with the prevailing base fares. 
 
o Non commissionable cruise Fare (NCCF/Port charges) will be added to 
the cruise Fare for certain markets and an indicato r will be returned as 
well. 
 
• Non-Refundable Promotions 
 
o Promotions can be classified as Refundable, Non-Ref undable Deposit and 
Non-Refundable Full Fare types. 
 
o Every promotion returned in the response will have Refundability type 
indicator. 
                                   1 - "No Restrict ions - Refundable" 
                                   2 - "Non-Refunda ble - Deposit" 
                                   3 - "Non-Refunda ble - Full Fare" 
 
o Refundable and Non-Refundable types will be include d in the response by 
default. Non-Refundable types can be excluded from the response by 
explicitly setting the “IncludeNonRefundablePromos”  Indicator to “No” 
along with each Fare/promotion. 
 
<SelectedFare  FareCode =" BESTRATE " IncludeNonRefundablePromos =" No "/> 
 
• Please see next subsection for category breakdown l ogic. 
 
14.1.2 Category List Response Breakdown Logic 
14.1.2.1  What are the status codes for each Category Code? 
The availability status of a category is indicated by the BreakdownType as shown below. 
14.1.2.2  How do I interpret the BreakdownTypes? 
The BreakdownType in the CategoryList response shou ld be interpreted as shown in the 
example below. 
(a) Single Occupancy Scenario Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 89 of 382 <alpha:PriceInfo  Amount =" 10580.00 " 
BreakdownType =" 0101C " NCCFAmount =" 400.00 " 
PromotionAmount =" 200 .00 "  PromotionClass =" 12 " "  
PromotionTypes =" 44 " FareCode =" FSTG01C " />     Cost of the Cruise Cabin for the first guest 
assuming single occupancy is 10580.00  (cruise 
+ NCCF) if TaxInclusive=”true” 
 
Total applied promotion Amount will be returned 
in PromotionAmount. 
 
Promotion Class(s) and Type(s) will be returned 
for applied discount(s) with a blank space 
delimiter. 
 
The first two characters in the BreakdownType 
indicate the occupany. In this case, since the 
BreakdownType value is "0101C", the first two 
characters "01" indicate single occupancy. 
 
The third and fourth characters indicate the 
specific guest's breakdown for the line item. In 
this case, since the BreakdownType value is 
"0101C", the third and fourth characters "01" 
indicate that the line item is for the first guest.  
 
The fifth character indicates the PriceType. If 
the value for the fifth character is "C", then the 
pricing is shown for Cabin. In situations, where 
the fifth character is "A", the pricing is for the Air 
Add on.   
 <alpha:PriceInfo  Amount =" 0" BreakdownType =" 0101A " 
FareCode =" FSTG01C " />   Since the value of the fifth character in the 
BreakdownType is "A", it is an Air Add on 
amount. Cost of the Air Add on for the first guest 
is 0 since it is a Cruise only booking 
 <alpha:PriceInfo  BreakdownType =" 01 A " 
FareCode =" FSTG01C " />   Since the availability is linked with the 
occupancy count, the third entry shows the 
availability and the occupancy. In this case, 
since the value of the BreakdownType is "01 A", 
it means that the category is available assuming 
single occupancy. A value of "W" indicates the 
status as Waitlisted while “C” means that the 
category is Closed. 
 
Also, notice that there is no Amount attribute 
included in this since this PriceInfo line item is 
used to indicate only the status and the 
occupancy associated with the status 
 <alpha:PriceInfo  BreakdownType =" 01 " 
FareCode =" FSTG01C " />   The fourth entry is a guarantee indicator

availability and the occupancy. In this case, 
since the value of the BreakdownType is "02 A", 
it means that the category is available assuming 
double occupancy. A value of "W" indicates the 
status as Waitlisted while “C” means that the 
category is Closed. 
 
Also, notice that there is no Amount attribute 
included in this since this PriceInfo line item is 
used to indicate only the status and the 
occupancy associated with the status 
<alpha:PriceInfo  BreakdownType =" 02 " 
FareCode =" FSTG01C " />   The fourth entry is a guarantee indicator 
 
14.1.2.3  Category location missing in some CategoryOptions? 
The Category Location will not have a value for vir tual categories normally named as 
"W","X","Y" and "Z".  These virtual categories are used for guarantees and will include 
inventory from multiple physical categories. Due to  this, it is not possible to provide a 
single value for the Category Location attribute. D ue to this fact, the Category Location 
attribute will not be present for virtual categorie s. 
14.1.2.4  Why do I get category/occupancy entries with FIT fa re code 
when I specified fare code XXX? 
When using a particular fare code other than LAF (d efault), there might be some 
categories where the given fare code does not apply .  These are returned with the FIT fare 
code.  FIT Pricing concept is no longer applicable after Pricing and promotions 
enhancement. FIT pricing is now replaced by prevail ing base fares. 
14.1.2.5  Rates are zero for most Rate codes? 
The Amounts shown in the response will always be ze ro for Air Add on line items for a 
cruise only booking.  The Amounts shown will also b e zero when a category is 
unavailable for booking.  Also, keep in mind that n ot all categories apply for a given 
promo code.  Therefore, if a promo code is provided  as part of the request, this behavior 
will also be seen when a category does not particip ate in the promotion. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

14.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Category List request and re sponse are 
OTA_CruiseCategoryAvailRQ and OTA_CruiseCategoryAva ilRS.  Our implementation 
is based on the OTA_2007A schema specification.

14.4.4 Use Case 
John decided to sail on the Radiance of the Seas on  June 17, 2011. He has selected a 
sailing that requires the payment of gratuities as a mandatory booking component.  
Because the advisory and the PPGR indicator is set to "A" the partner system will know 
to apply the gratuties to the booking for John, all owing him to get accurate pricing in the Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 99 of 382 booking process and allowing the booking to be crea ted with the gratuities. Jonh’s 
stateroom preference is accessible only. All promot ional qualifiers are set for a double 
occupancy request. 
14.4.4.1  Sample Message Request – OTA_CruiseCategoryAvailRQ 
 
         <OTA_CruiseCategoryAvailRQ TimeStamp ="2010-10-05T08:03:04"  Target ="Test"  Version ="2.0"

            <POS> 
             …………. 
             </POS> 
            <Guest Code =”10”  Age =”35”  LoyaltyMembershipID ="729871052" > 
               <GuestTransportation Mode ="29"  Status ="36" > 
                  <GatewayCity LocationCode ="C/O" /> 
               </GuestTransportation> 
               <Address> 
                  <StateProv StateCode ="FL" />  
               </Address> 
               <FareQualifiers FareRestriction ="1" /> 
 <FareQualifiers FareRestriction ="5" />

14.5 Error Handling 
Please refer error code appendix for a list of OTA error codes.   Note – At this time, OTA 
is yet to provide a numbering scheme for Cruise err or codes. 
14.6 Special Design Considerations 
• In the request, status code in GuestTransportation is an OTA_CodeType (Code 
List Name = Status). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendi x for more information. 
• In the request, mode code in GuestTransportation is  an OTA_CodeType (Code 
List Name = Transportation Code). Refer to OTA_Code Types appendix for more 
information. 
• In the response, status code in FareCodeOption/Cate goryOptions/CategoryOption 
is an OTA_CodeType (Code List Name = Status). Refer  to OTA_CodeTypes 
appendix for more information. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 102 of 382  
15. Cruise Category List Message Version 2.0 
15.1 Functional Overview 
This service is a new alternative to Cruise Categor y List. This enhanced version of 
Category availability service is introduced to bett er format the category level pricing 
information and avoids redundant information. This service provides the capability to 
request for Best Rate and Best Value and also allow s price comparison. Price comparison 
can be requested by sending two rates in the reques t. 
In order to get the new version, same CategoryList operation can be invoked with a 
different version number. 
15.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• All functional aspects supported in Version 1.0 wil l be available in this version. 
 
• Additional Promotional Qualifiers will be supported  in the request. 
 
• In addition to the new qualifiers, message will now  support pricing comparison 
between two price points. 
 
o Best Rate can be obtained by sending ‘BESTRATE’ as the FareCode in 
SelectedFare. 
                  <SelectedFare FareCode =”BESTRATE” > 
 
o Best Value can be obtained by sending TBD as the Fa reCode in 
SelectedFare. 
                  <SelectedFare FareCode =”BVL” > 
 
o Top two Best Rate/Values can be obtained by sending  two SelectedFares 
nodes. 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”BESTRATE” > 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”BESTRATE” > 
 <or> 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”BVL”> 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”BVL”> 
 
o Specific prices can be obtained by sending the prom otions returned as part 
of FareAvailability search. 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”RESRT001” > 
 
o Price comparison can be obtained by sending two Far ecodes in the 
SearchQualifiers. 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”Price1” > 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”Price2” > 
 
o Pricing for combinable promotions can also be reque sted. 
<SelectedFare> 
     <SelectedPromotions PromotionCode =”Promotion1” > Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 103 of 382      <SelectedPromotions PromotionCode =”Promotion2” > 
</SelectedFare > 
 
o Non Refundable Promotions can be excluded. 
<SelectedFare FareCode =”Promotion1” IncludeNonRefundablePromos =”No” > 
 
• Only  occupancy specific pricing will be returned. 
 
• Multiple occupancy pricing requests can be accommod ated by sending multiple 
occupancy specific category requests. 
 
• Additional promotional attributes such as PriceId, PriceTypeId, PromotionClass, 
promotionType, PromotionDescription, PromotionAmoun t will be returned. 
 
• Markets that require cruise fare and NCCF consolida tion will receive the 
CruiseFare amount with NCCF included. An indicator will be returned at the 
sailing level as well. 
 
• Applications that present a single NCCF rate for di splay will need to understand 
the NCCF can vary at guest/category level. 
 
• Please see next subsection for category breakdown l ogic.

15.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Category List request and re sponse are 
OTA_CruiseCategoryAvailRQ and OTA_CruiseCategoryAva ilRS.  Our implementation 
is based on the OTA_2007A schema specification.

get availability for connecting and accessible stat erooms.

15.5 Error Handling 
Please refer error code appendix for a list of OTA error codes.   Note – At this time, OTA 
is yet to provide a numbering scheme for Cruise err or codes. 
15.6 Special Design Considerations 
• In the request, status code in GuestTransportation is an OTA_CodeType (Code 
List Name = Status). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendi x for more information. 
• In the request, mode code in GuestTransportation is  an OTA_CodeType (Code 
List Name = Transportation Code). Refer to OTA_Code Types appendix for more 
information. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 112 of 382 • In the request, Guest Code is an OTA_CodeType (Code  List Name = 
TPA_AQC). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix for more information. 
• In the request, FareRestrictions is an OTA_CodeType  (Code List Name = 
TPA_FAQ). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix for more information. 
• In the response, status code in FareCodeOption/Cate goryOptions/CategoryOption 
is an OTA_CodeType (Code List Name = Status). Refer  to OTA_CodeTypes 
appendix for more information. 
• In the response, priceTypeID is an OTA_CodeType (Co de List Name = 
Rate_Type). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix for mor e information. 
• In the response, DiscountType, PromotionClass, Prom otionType is an 
OTA_CodeType (Code List Name = Promotion_Class and Promotion_Type). 
Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix for more informatio n.  
 
16. Cruise Cabin List Message 
16.1 Functional Overview 
The Cabin List Request message requests a list of a vailable cabins for a selected category 
on a sailing. The sailing information is defined by  the departure date and ship. The fare 
code and the berthed and priced category codes shou ld be retained from the respective list 
message and provided as part of the Cabin List requ est.  
 
It is also possible to retrieve only those cabins t hat are connected to another cabin or 
request availability status for a specific cabin.  
 
The response message returns a list of cabins match ing the specified criteria, and will 
provide the location, features and measurement info rmation about the cabins. It will also 
provide information pertaining to connecting cabins  and their availability. 
 
16.1.1 Additional Services 
• Determines if the sailing is eligible for auto upgr ades 
 
• Validates the following: 
- Ship departure date 
- Fare category code 
- Currency code 
- Price program/promo code 
- Cabin number if supplied 
 
• Checks air availability for the requested gateways 
 
• Default system behavior is to automatically return cabins for auto-upgrades 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 113 of 382 o In case where an application does not want upgrades  to be returned, it 
should pass the following as part of the request: 
/OTA_CruiseCabinAvailRQ/SearchQualifiers/Status/[@S tatus= 19] 
 
• If auto upgrade is not in effect: 
- Validate the category / price code combination 
- Retrieves the cabin numbers 
o If the category is only waitlisted, it returns the OTA_CodeType 
equivalent for waitlist 
o If the category is only guaranteed, it returns the Cabin number as 
“GTY” 
o If the category is available, it returns a list of the best available 
cabins based on: 
• Required cabin capacity for the number of guests in  the booking, 
• Requested cabin attribute, if any, 
• Deck preference, if any. 
- Validate the waitlisted gateways 
 
• If auto upgrade is in effect: 
 
- Determine which categories are available 
 
- Calculates how many cabins of each available catego ry to return. 
      The distribution is based on the maximum numb er of cabins that can be 
      displayed divided by the number of categories  that are available.  
o If their results are evenly divided, then an equiva lent number of 
cabins are calculated for each category. 
o If the remainder is greater than the quotient, then  the number of 
cabins calculated for the highest category is maxim ized and an 
equivalent number of cabins equal to the quotient a re calculated for 
the remaining categories. 
o If the remainder is less or equal to the quotient, then the number of 
cabins calculated for the lowest category is minimi zed and an 
equivalent number of cabins equal to the quotient a re calculated for 
the remaining categories. 
o If the number of cabins that can be returned is les s than the number 
of available categories, then one cabin will be ret urned for each of 
the highest categories until the list is filled. 
 
- It retrieves the cabins for each category starting from the highest category 
to the lowest category.  
 
- In order to retrieve a list of connected cabins, th e CabinAttributeCode 
should be provided in the request with a value of “ 4”.  
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 114 of 382 - If any category does not have enough available cabi ns, the carry-over is 
added to the next lower category 
 
- If no cabins are found (including guarantees) or th e category is not 
available, the response contains an error message. 
 
- Cabin availability will be returned based on the ac cessible stateroom 
qualifiers in the request. Partners may choose to o pt out for the stateroom 
qualifiers. A mix of Accessible and non-accessible staterooms (top 3 
accessible staterooms followed by non- accessible s taterooms) will be 
returned in opt out scenario. 
 
- Fire Zone Limit: Cabin Availability will be managed  by limiting the berth 
capacity under the SOLAS (Safety Of Life At Sea) li mits for a given ship.

16.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cabin List request and response are  OTA_CruiseCabinAvailRQ and 
OTA_CruiseCabinAvailRS.  Our implementation is base d on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification. 
16.3.1 Cabin List Request  
16.3.1.1  Data Types and Reuse Chart 
Functional Components  Re -Use and Source of other 
OTA Constructs 
POS (Point Of Sale) POS_Type   
Guest GuestType  
SailingInfo SailingCategoryInfoType 
SelectedFare FareGroup (Uses) 
SearchQualifiers SearchQualifierType (Extends) 
16.3.1.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• SelectedCabin element inside SailingCategoryInfoTyp e is ignored. 
• DeckNumber is the only supported attribute in the S earchQualifierTypes. 
• Cabin detailed description information is provided through a second request with 
cabin number populated. 
• Package Code and Fare Code need to be provided when  checking Cabin 
Availability 
16.3.1.3  Extensions 
None  
16.3.2 Cabin List Response  
16.3.2.1  Data Types and Reuse Chart

Page 116 of 382 16.3.2.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• ShipName attribute will not be provided in the Sail ingInfo/ SelectedSailing/ 
CruiseLine element 
• The maximum number of cabins returned will be deter mined by business rules 
even though the schema allows the retrieval of up t o 99 cabins. 
16.3.2.3  Extensions 
None

16.4.4 Use Case 2 
Jennifer is interested in finding out a list of con nected cabins and accessible staterooms 
on the Rhapsody of the Seas for 13 Jan 2011 and sen ds the following request.

17. Cabin Detail Message 
17.1 Functional Overview 
The Cabin Detail Request message requests the locat ion, features and measurement 
information about a cabin. 
 
This transaction returns detailed information about  a selected cabin. Unlike other “detail” 
transaction responses, the information in this resp onse is not returned in free form text 
but as specific values for an extensive list of cab in attributes (i.e. - Cabin Location In or 
Out, Bed Type, Cabin Capacity, etc.).  
17.1.1 Additional Services 
None

18. Cruise Cabin Hold Message 
18.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Cabin Hold request message instructs the  RCL reservations system to put a 
temporary hold on selected cabin(s) for a short tim e interval.  Interval is currently set for 
fifteen minutes .  This allows the user time to gather additional in formation which is 
required to complete the booking without concern fo r losing the cabin.  The sailing is 
identified by the ship and departure date.  RCL cur rently allows up to four cabins to be 
held at a time. 
The response message indicates the status of each c abin for which a hold is requested and 
RCL trip protection recommendation.  It is conceiva ble in the case of a request 
containing multiple cabins, that the status might b e different for one or more cabins.  If 
the cabin hold request was successful, the response  will indicate the time when the cabin 
will be automatically released back into inventory as well as which data elements are 
required to complete the booking. 
RCL strongly recommends the use of the Cabin Releas e message when the agent no 
longer requires a previously held set of cabins and  before attempting to hold a new set of 
cabins with the Cabin Hold message. 
18.1.1 Transaction Services 
• Checks to make sure that the sailing exists. 
 
• Checks to make sure that the category is still avai lable. 
 
• Checks the availability of Guaranteed cabins.  
 
• Checks if cabin requested when only guarantees are allowed. 
 
• Checks availability of triple and quad bookings for  the category. 
 
• Checks if booking a single or double into a triple or quad cabin is allowed. 
 
• Checks to see if number of guest in booking exceeds  the cabin capacity. 
 
• Checks for valid upgrades. 
 
• Can hold up to 4 cabins in the same berthed categor y. 
 
• On a hold 
- Is it a valid cabin 
- Is cabin still available 
- Holds cabin for 15 minutes (current setting for RCL ) Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 136 of 382 • Note: This message no longer returns dining seating  status 
 
• Returns information on whether the addition of pre- paid gratuities needs to be 
enforced by API Partners. 
 
• Mandatory Prepaid Gratuities indicator will be retu rned in the response for 
sailings and market. The two possible values are “A ” – Automated and “M”-
Mandatory. 
 
• Accessible stateroom qualifiers will be accepted in  the request to identify the 
customer request for accessible/non-accessible stat erooms. Cabins requested will 
be validated against the qualifier received. Partne rs may choose to opt out for this 
qualifier. 
 
• Cabins can be held for group booking process. 
 
- Can hold cabins from general inventory when creatin g/amending 
Groups and Group Bookings. 
- Can hold cabins from Groups allocated inventory whe n 
creating/amending Group bookings. 
18.2 Typical Process Flow 
 
 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

18.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Cabin Hold request and respo nse are OTA_CruiseCabinHoldRQ 
and OTA_CruiseCabinHoldRS.  Our implementation is b ased on the OTA_2007A 
schema specification.  
18.3.1 Cruise Cabin Hold Request  
18.3.1.1  Data Types and Reuse Chart 
Functional Components  Re -Use and Source of other 
OTA Constructs

Guest GuestType 
SearchQualifiers SearchQualifierType ( Extends) 
 
18.3.1.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• RCL allows up to four cabins from a single sailing even though the schema allows 
cabins from up to three sailings to be held simulta neously.  All four cabins must 
be of the same cabin category for the same sailing.  
• RCL allows a maximum of four guests for which a cab in can be held for a single 
request even though the schema allows up to nine gu ests 
• RCL will ignore both currency parameters, both the currency 
OTA_CruiseCabinHoldRQ/Currency element and the ISOC urrency element in 
the POS structure.

• None

19. Cruise Cabin Release Message 
19.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Cabin Release request message is used to  release a hold that was previously 
placed on a cabin or cabins and send back into the available inventory. 
The response message indicates the status for the c abin in the request.  If unsuccessful, a 
warning or advisory message is returned. 
Group Reservations: 
o Cabin(s) held from general inventory will be releas ed back to the available 
inventory. 
o Cabin(s) held from groups pre-allocated inventory w ill be released back to group 
inventory allocation.  
19.1.1 Transaction Services 
• Immediately releases cabin held via a previous OTA_ CruiseCabinHold 
message.  
19.2 Typical Process Flow

20. Cruise Fare List Message 
20.1 Functional Overview 
 
This transaction returns a list of the promotional programs that are applicable to a 
selected ship, sail date, and other guest requireme nts. 
 
The Fare List Request message requests a listing of  available fares for a selected RCL 
sailing.  The ship and departure date identifies th e sailing. The guest count structure is 
used to communicate the number of guests that will be sailing.  Although Guest 
Transportation information is optional, in normal p ractice it is advisable to enter the 
mode of transportation and gateway city because som e fares have restrictions based on 
transportation. 
The response message returns a list of all fares an d promotions, including agency specific 
restricted fares, for which the traveler qualifies based upon the criteria provided. 
Additionally, it returns the taxes and fees applica ble for the given sailing. 
20.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Only returns promos that are compatible with each g uests’ air city when provided 
 
• Only returns promos that are compatible with the se lected package when provided 
 
• When a package is associated with a promotional pro gram, it checks the 
availability of the components of that package. 
 
• If package ID is not included in the request, the “ Just a Cruise” (JAC) default 
package ID for the ship and departure date will be used to retrieve the details.  
 
• Number of occurences of guest node is used as the o ccupancy 
 
• GuestTransportation/@Mode needs to be set to 29 for  C/O bookings. It needs to 
be set to 14 for Air. If set to 14, then GatewayCit y is required 
 
• Even though CruisePackageCode is optional for JAC p ackages, it is required for 
cruisetours/ non-JAC packages 
 
• Returns only effective fare codes when the 
/OTA_CruiseFareAvailRQ/SearchQualifiers/Status/@Sta tus attribute is provided. 
Response will include closed fare codes when Status  node not included as part of 
the request. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 145 of 382 • Returns Prices and promotions specific to Groups an d Group Reservations as 
well. 
 
• Pricing and Promotions 
 
o Additional Guest Level promotional qualifiers will be accepted. Based on 
the input qualifiers the system will return the eli gible list of promotion 
codes. 
 
o The list of promotion codes would include the liter al ‘BESTRATE’, 
‘BVL’-BestValue, base price definitions, and promot ions. 
 
o Lowest Available Fare (LAF) is now referred as BEST RATE.  
 
o Promotion combinability information can be requeste d by setting 
“IncludeCombinability” flag in the request. 
 
o All promotions will be returned in the response wit h the flag indicating the 
eligibility based on the input promotional qualifie rs. 
 
o Loyalty and Coupon code based prmotions will be ret urned only when  
valid Guest level qualifiers are set. 
 
• Non-Refundable Promotions 
 
o Promotions can be classified as Refundable, Non-Ref undable Deposit and 
Non-Refundable Full Fare types. 
 
o Every promotion returned in the response will have Refundability type 
indicator. 
                                   1 - "No Restrict ions - Refundable" 
                                   2 - "Non-Refunda ble - Deposit" 
                                   3 - "Non-Refunda ble - Full Fare" 
 
o Refundable and Non-Refundable types will be include d in the response by 
default. Non-Refundable types can be excluded from the response by 
explicitly setting the “IncludeNonRefundablePromos”  Indicator to “No”. 
 
<TPA_FareType  IncludeNonRefundablePromos =" No "/>  
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

Name = Promotion_Type). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appe ndix for more 
information.

22. Cruise Booking Price Message 
22.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Booking Price request message requests t he pricing for all components of a 
booking.  All of the components to be purchased mus t be included in the Cruise Booking 
Price request. This includes the sailing by using e ither the booking id or the ship and sail 
date, the priced and berthed category, the fare cod e, the gateway, the pre and/or post land 
packages, special services, bus transfers, inclusiv e packages, insurance, and available 
dining sitting. 
The response message returns the pricing breakdown by component for both the booking 
and each guest. In addition to this, this message r eturns an accurate and comprehensive 
breakdown of the prices, commission amounts and com mission percentages by guest for 
each component in a booking. 
 
In amend mode, the client must provide the existing  passenger ids for the given booking 
so that the repricing can take place within the pri cing rules at booking creation.  
Otherwise, RCL will price assuming new passengers.  Please use 
//ContactInfo/@GuestRefNumber to provide the existi ng passenger ids. 
 
When in amend mode, if the existing booking has air  booked via Choice Air, the air 
amount will be returned at the passenger level.  Th e amount will be qualified by a price 
type code of 7 – deviation charge. ( //PriceInfo/@P riceTypeCode = “7”).  A passenger’s 
air provider information will determine whether the  passenger has Choice Air. 
(//ProviderInfo/Provider == ‘CHOICE AIR’). 
 
Also in amend mode,  all guest details returned as a part of the booking retrieval response 
message should be sent in the request unless a book ing change is desired. Any guests not 
included in the request message would be presumed t o have been dropped from the 
booking. While providing the guest detail values in  the request is optional, all available 
values should be supplied in the request in order t o prevent business rule validation 
failures for some guest detail elements later on in  the booking process.  
 
Note:  Cruise Booking Retrieval returns detailed pricing information only when explicitly 
requested.  The partner can also call this message if they require detailed pricing 
information as part of their application flow. 
 
Pricing will return a line item for all price type codes that are part of the booking. 
Partners should display all components that are rel evant.  
 
 
22.1.1 Transaction Services 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 159 of 382 • All components are checked for validity and availab ility (when appropriate). 
These components include; 
- The agency 
- The desired currency 
- The ship 
- The departure date 
- The package code 
- The price program 
- The dining seating 
- The category  of actual cabin being requested (Cabi n category) 
- The category of cabin at which the pricing is being  requested (Rate 
Category) 
- The cabin number 
- Trip Insurance  
- Guest Details 
- Air transportation gateways 
- Tours 
- Options such as Aqua spa with an associated price 
- Buses 
- Cruise Only Transfers 
- Dining 
- Guest Level Promotional qualifiers 
 
• This transaction will completely re-price a booking .  In amend mode, it will 
retrieve the previously assigned prices for booking  components that have not 
changed and obtain new pricing for those components  that have changed as 
long as the existing passenger ids are provided. 
 
• The transaction calculates and returns summary amou nts for:   
- Other charge items (this includes the options, tour s, air deviations and 
cruise only transfers) 
- Tariff charges, which includes the cabin, air, NCCF  (Non Commissionable 
Cruise Fare), and taxes. 
- Total commissions 
 
• The transaction calculates and returns payment item s including 
- The require deposit amount 
- Amount Received 
- Balance due 
- Payment Amount 
 
• The SelectedDining/@Status attribute needs to be pr ovided with either a 
Confirmed or Waitlisted value in order to process t he pricing request 
successfully.  
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 160 of 382 • FlightInformation although present and conformant w ith the XML schema is 
not validated or used as a part of this service. Ho wever including this 
information as-is from the booking retrieval respon se will not impact the 
pricing transaction. 
 
• Components will not be priced when in waitlisted st atus. Cruise only transfers 
with required flight information will be priced whe n Air information is sent as 
part of the selectedPackages. 
 
• Dining is not validated for accuracy. However if My Time dining is selected as 
confirmed dining or as a waitlisted dining along wi th another confirmed 
dining for the same guest, pre paid gratuities will  be automatically added in 
the pricing response.  
 
• Element Profiles under GuestDetails will be ignored . However, sending this 
information from the prior booking retrieval will n ot impact the pricing 
transaction. 
 
• Auto Add functionality will include automatically a dding charges to the 
reservations. The evaluation and application of aut o added charges will be 
based on the eligibility at the time of pricing in shopping, creation and 
amending the reservation. Removal of Nonmandatory a uto add charge is also 
supported. 
 
• User preference for Accessible/Non-Accessible state room will be accepted in 
the request. Stateroom in the request will be valid ated against the qualifier. 
Partners may choose to opt out for the qualifier. 
 
• Pricing and Promotions 
 
o Retrieve Pricing  - In Amend mode, booking asis  pricing can be 
requested by passing the booking id and a “Retrieve Price” action code. 
 
o Sailing and guest level promotional qualifiers will  derive the best 
available promotions. 
 
o In pricing amend mode, all promotional qualifiers a re expected back in 
the request (unless explicitly changed by the agent ) to retain any 
applied restricted promotional discounts. 
 
o Pricing can be requested with the following pricing  options; 
 
• BESTRATE – Best rate will be applied based on the i nput 
promotional qualifiers. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 161 of 382 • BVL – Best Value will be applied based on the input  qualifiers. If 
Best Value is not applicable for the sailing, BESTR ATE will be 
returned. 
 
• Base Price Id/ Lead Promotion ID – returns pricing for base price 
id or Lead promotion id with any applicable combina ble 
promotions. 
 
• List of Promotions with or without Lead Promotion I D – returns 
pricing with the combination set requested based on  the eligiblity. 
 
• Non-Refundable Promotions 
 
o Promotions can be classified as Refundable, Non-Ref undable Deposit and 
Non-Refundable Full Fare types. 
 
o Every promotion returned in the response will have Refundability type 
indicator. 
                                   1 - "No Restrict ions - Refundable" 
                                   2 - "Non-Refunda ble - Deposit" 
                                   3 - "Non-Refunda ble - Full Fare" 
 
o Bookings will be marked as NonRefundable, if it had /has Non-Refundable 
promotions during the booking lifecycle. This indic ator will be identified 
as Greatest Refundability type and will be returned  as 
BookingNonRefundableType in booking retrieval, pricing and 
confirmation responses. 
 
o Refundable and Non-Refundable types will be include d in the response by 
default. Non-Refundable types can be excluded from the response by 
explicitly setting the “IncludeNonRefundablePromos”  Indicator to “No”.

22.4.3 Use Case 
22.4.3.1  Sample Message Request  
John and a guest have decided to sail on the Freedo m of the Seas on August 2, 2009 and 
wants to price cabin 1289 in category L using promo  code BRK07.  The booking will be 
cruise only, they have selected traveler coverage, and have selected the ‘M’ flexible 
dining sitting from the Cruise Dining List message response.  
<m:getBookingPrice  xmlns:m =" http://services.rccl.com/Interfaces/BookingPrice ">

22.4.3.3  Sample Message Request  
 
After creating the booking with id 15363, a few cha nges are made to the booking with Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 170 of 382 many different components in confirmed and waitlist ed status. Most of the relevant 
information from GuestDetails Node can be returned as is from the booking retrieval 
response message if there are no changes to the inf ormation. Please note that information 
sent in the request is validated based on business rules defined for certain scenarios. 
Presence of data does not automatically ensure vali dation. 
 
The booking re-price message is sent below with cha nges to booking 15363. 
 
<OTA_CruisePriceBookingRQ RetransmissionIndicator=" false" SequenceNmbr="1" TimeStamp="2009-12-
14T15:11:20.407Z" Version="1.0" xmlns="http://www.o pentravel.org/OTA/2003/05/alpha"> 
            <POS> 
             ………….. 
            </POS>

21.4.3.7 Auto Add Options  
 
 
Mandatory Auto Add Charges: 
During the price booking process the mandatory charges will be retained in the booking 
irrespective of the guest preference. 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " /> 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " SelectedOptionsIndicator =" true " /> 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " SelectedOptionsIndicator =" false " /> 
< ** FUEL option is not sent back in the request **  /> 
 
In all the above cases the item will be included in the pricing. 
 
Non-Mandatory Auto Add Charges: 
During the pricing booking process the non-mandatory charges will be retained in the 
booking unless the explicit opt out is specified. 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " SelectedOptionsIndicator =" true" /> 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " /> 
< ** FUEL option is not sent back in the request **  /> 
 
In all the above cases the item will be included in the pricing. 
Non-mandatory charges can be opted out by explicating setting th e 
selectedOptionIndicator to “False”. 
 
< SelectedOptions OptionCode =" FUEL " SelectedOptionsIndicator =" false " /> 
If “false” is sent the item will not be included in the pricin g response. This 
declined item can only be added back by back office process by calli ng in. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

23. Cruise Validate Linked Bookings Message 
23.1 Functional Overview 
The Validate Linked Bookings Request message is use d to validate the cross reference 
booking numbers for all the categories – Tours, Din ing, and Air. 
The response will include, next to each booking id being linked, a ‘Y’ or ‘N’ stating 
whether the link was successfully created or not.  Please see sample response for more 
details. 
23.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Validates whether 
/square4 The bookings are valid 
/square4 The bookings are in the same sailing 
 
• Links up to 8 valid bookings per link type: 
o Dining – OTA LTC code 2 
o Tour ( Hotels) – OTA LTC code 3 
o Air – OTA LTC code 6 
23.2 Typical Process Flows 
RCCL Partner 
Set Booking Cross Reference Booking Retrieval
Booking Cross Reference Guest Details 
/ OTA_CruisePriceBookingRQ

/ OTA_CruiseBookRS
