25. Cruise Confirm Booking Message 
25.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Confirm Booking message is used to creat e a booking, amend a booking or 
cancel a booking on the RCL reservation system for a specific sailing, with a specified 
mode of transportation/gateway city pair and curren cy, and a selected fare/category pair, 
for one or more passengers in a specific cabin. 
Prior to submitting a Confirm Booking request messa ge, a cabin must have been placed 
on hold.  The only exception to this is if a cabin is reserved as a guarantee, rather than a 
specific cabin. If a booking transaction is not com pleted when the cabin is held, it can 
still be booked if it is available at the time of t he booking request receipt. In case the 
cabin is not available, then an error is sent back to select a new cabin. 
The response message indicates if the request was s uccessful and returns a Reservation 
ID number. 
 
In amend mode, the client must provide the existing  passenger ids for the given booking. 
Please use //ContactInfo/@GuestRefNumber to provide  the existing passenger ids. 
 
This transaction performs the following functions: 
 
• It is a comprehensive general-purpose validation pr ogram that can check the 
validity and availability of all the components tha t have been selected for a 
booking. If errors are found, the process stops and  the appropriate error message 
is returned in the response.   
 
• If all the components are valid and the request ind icates that the booking should 
be confirmed, the transaction program will confirm the new or amended booking 
by recording the changes in the RCL reservation sys tem.  
 
• If the credit card details are entered here and all  the input fields are validated, the 
credit card payment will be applied to the booking.  
 
• Cruise Booking Amend is similar to creating a booki ng except that the 
Reservation ID is already available.  
 
• The first guest is always considered to be the prim ary guest. In situations where 
there is a need to change the primary guest associa ted with a booking, the details 
of the guest who should be designated as the primar y contact for a booking should 
be sent first in the booking confirm or amend reque sts. 
 
• For travel partners operating in USA and Canada, a mobile contact and email 
address will be required for the first guest in the  reservation, by no later than the Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 190 of 382 due date for final payment. This information will b e captured as part of First 
Guest  Alternate address contact. 
 
• It is possible to provide a booking to link to when  the booking is created or 
amended. However, the booking link is only a reques t and does not guarantee that 
the guests on the linked bookings will dine or fly together. 
 
• SelectedSailing/@Status of 60 instructs RCL to hand le the amendment as a cruise 
reschedule 
 
• During the confirm booking process the mandatory ch arges will be retained in the 
booking irrespective of the guest preference. the n on-mandatory charges will be 
retained in the booking unless the explicit opt out  is specified.  Non-mandatory 
charges can be opted out by explicly setting settin g the selectedOptionIndicator to 
“False”.  If “false” is sent the item will be remov ed from the booking. 
Confirmation response will have the updated pricing  information. This declined 
item can only be added back by back office process by calling in.  Additional 
information about auto add charges will be returned  in Guest Level pricing. 
 
• Accessible stateroom qualifiers will be accepted in  the request. Customer 
preference for accessible/non-accessible staterooms  will be stored. Partners may 
choose to opt out for the qualifier input. 
 
• Pricing and Promotions 
 
o Guest level promotional qualifiers are accepted.   
 
o Promotional qualifiers are required to price and co nfirm restricted 
promotions. 
 
o Lowest Available Fare (LAF) is now being replaced w ith Best Rate 
(BESTRATE).  
 
o Best Available Offer concept (BVL-BestValue) is als o being introduced.  
 
o Promotional Qualifiers are required both in create and amend mode for 
restricted promotions. 
 
o In booking amend mode, all promotional qualifiers s et at the guest level is 
expected back in the request (unless explicitly cha nged by the agent) to 
retain any applied restricted promotional discounts . 
 
o Booking confirmation can be requested with the foll owing pricing 
combinations; 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 191 of 382 • BESTRATE – Best rate will be applied based on the i nput 
promotional qualifiers. 
 
• BVL – Best Value will be applied based on the input  qualifiers. If 
Best Value is not applicable for the sailing, BESTR ATE will be 
returned. 
 
• Base Price Id/ Lead Promotion ID – Booking will be confirmed 
with base price id or Lead promotion id with any ap plicable 
combinable promotions. 
 
• List of Promotions with or without Lead Promotion I D – Booking 
will be confirmed with the combination set requeste d based on the 
eligiblity. 
 
• Guest Pre-vacation contact 
 
- For travel partners operating in USA and Canada, a mobile contact and 
email address will be required for the first guest in the reservation, by 
no later than the due date for final payment. This information will be 
returned as part of First Guest  Alternate address contact. 
 
• Non-Refundable Promotions 
 
o Promotions can be classified as Refundable, Non-Ref undable Deposit and 
Non-Refundable Full Fare types. 
 
o Every promotion returned in the response will have Refundability type 
indicator. 
                                   1 - "No Restrict ions - Refundable" 
                                   2 - "Non-Refunda ble - Deposit" 
                                   3 - "Non-Refunda ble - Full Fare" 
 
o Bookings will be marked as NonRefundable, if it had /has Non-Refundable 
promotions during the booking lifecycle. This indic ator will be identified 
as Greatest Refundability type and will be returned  as 
BookingNonRefundableType in booking retrieval, pricing and 
confirmation responses. 
 
o Refundable and Non-Refundable types will be include d in the response by 
default. Non-Refundable types can be excluded from the response by 
explicitly setting the “IncludeNonRefundablePromos”  Indicator to “No”. 
 
<SelectedCategory  PricedCategoryCode =" Q" BerthedCategoryCode =" Q" IncludeNonRefundablePromos =" No " 
FareCode =" B7227949 ">  
 
• Global Guest Data  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 192 of 382 o In Language guest level attributes such as first na me, last name and 
middle name will be captured and maintained for Chi nese markets.  
25.1.1 Transaction Services 
In amend mode, the system: 
 
• Applies the following defaults: 
- If the package code is blank, the package code “jus t a cruise” is defaulted. 
- If the promo code that is requested is “LAF” (lowes t available fare) / 
BESTRATE (Best Rate), the application automatically  finds the lowest 
available fare code associated with the guests othe r selections.  However, 
RCL strongly recommends using the specific promo co de used in the Pricing 
message since LAF can change during the booking pro cess. 
- If the selected package includes tours, the reserva tion system will validate 
that the selected tour does not conflict with the p ackage. 
- If a guest is removed from the booking, any couple dependent special 
services (anniversary and honeymoon) will be droppe d and a warning 
message will be returned. 
 
• All components are checked for validity and availab ility (when appropriate). 
These components include; 
- The agency 
- The desired currency 
- The ship 
- The departure date 
- The package identifier 
- The price program 
- The category  of actual cabin being requested (Cabi n category) 
- The category of cabin at which the pricing is being  requested (Rate 
Category) 
- The cabin number 
- Trip Insurance  
- Guest Details 
- Air transportation gateways 
- Tours 
- Special Services 
- Options 
- Buses 
- Cruise Only Transfers 
- Guest Level promotional qualifiers 
 
• If the components are valid and the confirmation is  requested, the transactions 
records all the components in RCL’s reservation sys tem and returns a 
confirmation number that will be used to reference the booking in all subsequent 
activity. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 193 of 382 • Generally, all new bookings confirmed by this trans action will be in offered 
status. When a payment is applied to the reservatio n, the status will then change to 
confirmed once the payment has been posted. 
 
• Certain agencies may be able to indicate that booki ng payment will be done with 
a bank check. 
25.2 Typical Process Flow 
RCCL Partner 
Request Cabin Hold 
Cabin Hold / OTA_CruiseCabinHoldRQ 
Cabin Held / OTA_CruiseCabinHoldRS 
Cabin Pricing / OTA_CruisePriceBookingRQ 
Cabin Pricing Detail/ OTA_CruisePriceBookingRS 
Cruise Booking / OTA_CruiseBookRQ 
Booking Confirmation / OTA_CruiseBookRS 
 
 
 
25.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Confirm Booking request and response are OTA_CruiseBookRQ 
and OTA_CruiseBookRS.  Our implementation is based on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 194 of 382 25.3.1 Cruise Confirm Booking Request  
25.3.1.1  Data Types and Reuse Chart 
Functional Components  Re -Use and Source of other 
OTA Constructs 
POS POSType 
SailingInfo SailingCategoryInfoType 
ReservationInfo CruiseGuestInfoType 
25.3.1.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• Maximum of 8 valid Booking Cross Reference IDs’ are  allowed for each cross-
reference type for a reservation. 
• ReservationInfo/ReservationID is intended to be use d for RCL Reservation ID 
only.  PNRs are not supported. 
• Deleted guest element is ignored. 
• Selected fare code will be read from the SelectedCa tegory node.  All others will 
be ignored. 
• Combinable promotion set can be sent in SelectedCat egory/SelectedPromotions 
node. 
• In Guest Detail, one guest transportation value nee ds to be in confirmed status.  
Optionally, the second occurrence might be a waitli st. 
• In Guest Detail, one Selected Dining needs to be in  confirmed status.  Optionally, 
the second occurrence might be a waitlist. 
• Upto five fare qualifiers can be set per guest. 
• Only one coupon code can set in SelectedOffers node  per guest. 
• Only one occurrence of Loyalty Info is supported pe r guest. 
• Only one occurrence of Selected Insurance is suppor ted per guest. 
• A maximum of four Selected Special Services per gue st is supported. 
25.3.1.3  Extensions 
• None

25.3.2.2  Constraints and Restrictions 
• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• The summary totals need to be computed by the partn er based on the individual 
amounts provided as a part of the response message.  
• ReservationID is intended to be used for RCL Reserv ation ID only.  PNRs are not 
supported. 
25.3.2.3  Extensions 
• None

25.4.3 Use Case 
John and Mary Traveler have decided to go on the Fr eedom of the Seas for a 7 night 
cruise sailing on 2009-08-02. They have decided tha t they want cabin 1382 in category 
D1 and the agent has selected the BRK307 promo code .  They have provided their 
passport information and selected E-docs for docume ntation delivery and have also 
selected pre-paid gratuities and insurance.  Additi onally, they are reserving a post cruise 
tour and selected Los Angeles and Dallas as their a ir gateways.  Their neighbors are Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 200 of 382 already booked on the same sailing with booking id 1112223 and John has asked RCL to 
link their dining reservations so that they can din e together. 
 
Note: The payment node is included only as an examp le.  The sample response does not 
reflect that a payment has been applied to the book ing in question.

selectedOptionIndicator to “False”.

25.6 Special Design Considerations 
• As you design your client application, please take in consideration the fact that 
this is a resource intensive operation and its resp onse time can be considerable. 
The current Service Level Agreement (SLA) states th at the average response time Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 207 of 382 shall be around 3 seconds. This transaction might t ake longer than the average 
response time. This response time however does not include network delays 
introduced on the internet that are outside of RCL’ s control.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 208 of 382  
26. Cruise Guest Option List Message 
26.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Guest Option List message is used to obt ain the list of guest options available 
on a given sailing. The list of options eg. Spa, ma ssage therapy that are returned as part of 
this message are fee-based.  
 
The response includes the list of options available  for that sailing, including the option 
price and cthe charge type.  The charge type is def ined by OTA code CHG and is 
typically ‘7’ or ‘Per Person’. 
26.2 Typical Process Flow  
 
 
 
Partner RCCL 
Booking Summary 
/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ Options RetrievalBooking Retrieval
Special Services Retrieval/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ 
Option Detail/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ 
Special Services/Options List
Options Detail/ OTA_ResRetrieveRS 
 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 209 of 382 26.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Cruise Guest Service List request a nd response are 
OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ and OTA_CruiseSpeci alServiceAvailRS.  Our 
implementation is based on the OTA_2007A schema spe cification.

Page 212 of 382 27. Cruise Guest Service List Message 
27.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Guest Service List message is used to ob tain the list of guest services 
available for a given sailing.  
 
Guest services include anniversaries, birthdays, wh eelchair assistance, special dietary 
needs, onboard language preference, and are non mon etary in nature. 
 
Guest Services are offered at either a passenger or  cabin level, with the cabin being 
anoptional element in the message request. 
 
27.2 Typical Process Flow  
 
 
 
Partner RCCL 
Booking Summary 
/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ Options RetrievalBooking Retrieval
Special Services Retrieval/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ 
Option Detail/ OTA_CruiseSpecialServiceAvailRQ 
Special Services/Options List
Options Detail/ OTA_ResRetrieveRS 
 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

29. Cruise Fast Sell Message 
29.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Fast Sell message requires the partner t o provide the mandatory ship and sail 
date information. Optionally, category, price progr am, package code, and cabin 
information may be provided. The Guest Transportati on Type and City can also be 
specified at each passenger level. However, instead  of upgrade codes, the priced and 
berthed codes can be supplied in the request. 
  
29.1.1 Transaction Services 
The Fast Sell message is a multi-purpose request to  access one of the following cruise 
provider services: 
 
• The FastSell message allows up to four cabins to be  held and booked in a single 
request. 
  
• Cabin Availability List when no cabins are held.  T his could be due to 
unavailability of the cabin(s) requested, invalid c abin number(s) requested, or 
cabin number(s) missing in the request.  A valid ca tegory must be provided. 
 
• Category List when category is not provided or inva lid and a valid fare code is 
provided 
 
• Fare availability when fare code is not provided or  invalid and a valid sailing 
(optionally inclusive package) is provided 
 
• Package List when the package is specified, but not  available or invalid for the 
sailing 
 
• Sailing List when the sailing specified is invalid or unavailable. 
 
• Accessible stateroom qualifiers will be accepted in  the request.  
 
• Pricing and Promotions 
 
o The service request will accept optional promotion eligibility qualifiers at 
the guest level.  
 
o A fast sell request without qualifiers will be elig ible for unrestricted 
promotions. 
 
• Non-Refundable Promotions Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 222 of 382  
o The service request will accept optional filter to exclude Non-Refundable 
promotions. 
 
o Reponse will return the Refundable type indicator w herever it is 
applicable.  
 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

30. Cruise Make Payment Message 
30.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Make Payment message processes one credi t card payment at a time and 
returns a confirmation to the partner.  
30.1.1 Transaction Services 
• Based on the applicable business rules, credit card  payment may not be allowed 
for a booking. 
 
• The client entering the payment information must be  authorized to pay with credit 
cards prior to the application of payments. 
 
• Invalid credit card types will be rejected.  The RC L_CruiseLogin message 
provides a list of valid credit cards for the partn er/agency. 
 
• Based on the client workflow, PaymentEligibility me ssage should be used to get 
details on payment schedules and installment paymen ts that are allowed for a 
particular agency. Brazilian market is the only mar ket that supports installment 
payment currently.  
 
• A successful validation of the credit card consists  of RCL performing a real-time 
online credit card authorization. 
30.2 Typical Process Flow 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

31. Cruise Itinerary Detail Message 
31.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Cruise Itinerary Detail message is used to retu rn the itinerary details of the 
sailing.The message allows travel customers to requ est the detailed itinerary for a 
specific sailing. 
 
The request message accepts a ship and sail date to  retrieve the itinerary.  
 
The response message contains the detailed itinerar y in the format below: 
 
/square4 Every location the ship visits in its entire sailin g is listed as a port on the 
itinerary. 
/square4 The departure date and time are listed for each por t except the disembarkation 
port. 
/square4 The arrival date and time are listed for each port except the embarkation port. 
/square4 The port element can also specify “At Sea”, indicat ing a sailing period. 
/square4 Each port listed contains an indicator to specify w hether the ship docks at that 
specific location. This feature can be employed to include scenic locations 
such as “The Great Barrier Reef” on the itinerary, even though the ship does 
not dock at the location. 
Each port and its code listed also contains an indi cator to specify whether or not a 
shore excursion exists at that location. 
There is no sorting of the results since the itiner ary is based on each day of the 
sailing.  
Note: This message does not return a given port’s c ountry code.  It is up to the 
partner to map ports to countries if required by th e partner’s system. 
31.1.1 Transaction Services 
• Returns the itinerary details associated with the s ailing .  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 234 of 382 31.2 Typical Process Flow

32. Cruise Booking Document Message 
32.1 Functional Overview 
The Cruise Booking Document message provides the us er the ability to request a 
document type and its delivery method without retri eving the reservation. Normally, e-
docs are available if the sailing date is at least 30 days in the future from the time of 
booking. 
 
32.1.1 Transaction Services 
The user can specify in the request the reservation  ID and the type of document (see chart 
below) the user wants along with the optional deliv ery details – email or fax number.  
 
• In case the recipient information is not provided, the RCL Cruise API default 
rules are applied for sending reservation documenta tion and is driven by the given 
agency configuration. 
• The delivery method will be determined by whetner t he phone or email elements 
are provided as part of the request if present. 
• Possible values for 
/OTA_CruiseBookingDocumentRQ/CruiseDocument/Recipie ntInfo/@ContactTy 
pe are 
o AGENT 
o GUEST 
o BOTH 
• The bookings that can be requested at any time depe nd on the status of the 
booking. Some of the criteria based on which the li st of documents can be 
requested are given below: 
 
Document Name Document 
Type Code Criteria when document can be requested 
Booking Invoice  6 Can be requested after a booking is created and p rior to 
sailing  
APIS Letter  8 Can be requested when the booking has a valid 
agreement status  
Cancellation Invoice  11 Can be requested when the following criteria are  met 
• Booking status is "CX"

33. Retrieve Booking Message 
33.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Retrieve Booking message uses the RCL booking i d to retrieve the components 
of a booking, to include cruise, air details, and t our information. 
The response also includes information related to a ir booked via Choice Air. 
 
33.2 Transaction Services 
• This transaction puts a lock on the booking so that  no other client can retrieve 
or update the booking while the current client is u pdating it.  
- This hold will remain in effect for a short duratio n currently set at 15 
minutes. 
 
• This transaction returns a set of flags (the bookin g matrix) to indicate what 
types of changes are allowed on the booking.  
- Restrictions are based on factors such as the lengt h of time to the 
departure date, documents already issued, payment s tatus, etc. 
 
- When code 77 is returned under the NotModifiable cr uise profile, the 
booking cannot be ammended via the Cruise API.  Thi s is due to the 
booking having a segmented/ interporting itinerary or taking part in 
back-to-back bookings.  At this point, the booking is only returned for 
informational purposes only. 
 
- RCL recommends that the partner’s client applicatio n leverage the 
provided booking restrictions to control the amendm ent navigation 
before submitting additional transaction requests t o the API. 
 
• The response will provide air details if the bookin g includes air, assignment 
and viewable status, and Choice Air details. 
 
• Full pricing details are not available for default retrieval request.  Detailed 
Pricing can received by setting the Request in “Ret rievePrice” Mode.  
 
• Customer request for accessible/non-accessible stat eroom qualifier and 
additional cabin related information will be return ed. If partners choose to opt 
out for the qualifiers in the confirmBooking reques t, default qualifier value 
will be assigned based on the confirmed stateroom. 
 
• Choice Air scenarios 
/square4 When a passenger has booked air via Choice Air Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 243 of 382 • A passenger’s //ProviderInfo/Provider will specify ‘CHOICE 
AIR’ 
• //@PriceTypeCode = 161 shows the penalty amount whe n a 
guest cancelled their Choice Air booking and is 0 w hen 
component is not cancelled.  Needs to be displayed as "Choice 
Air penalty amount" when provided. 
• //@PriceTypeCode = 162 shows the penalty amount tha t has 
been deducted from the payments already made to the  booking 
and is only used to determine amount due.  Does not  need to be 
displayed. 
• //@PriceTypeCode = 161 - 162 > 0 shows the penalty amount 
due.  Needs to be displayed as "Choice Air penalty amount 
due" when > 0. 
• //@PriceTypeCode = 163 shows the actual cost for th e Choice 
Air component.  Shows 0 when cancelled.  Needs to b e 
displayed as "Choice Air charge/cost"  
• Passenger level Choice Air service charge is return ed in 
//@PriceTypeCode = 164 and is not required to be di splayed 
on the pricing display screen. 
• Secure flight data will be returned in the GuestDet ails node 
under the ContactInfo XML element. The new attribut es that 
will be returned will be MiddleNameFlag, RedressNum ber,  
KnownTravelerNumber.  
• Operating carrier Name will be returned.

summary of choice air pricing details plus the book ing invoice.

contact and email address will be required for the first guest in 
the reservation, by no later than the due date for final payment. 
This information will be returned as part of First Guest  
Alternate address contact.

o Promotion and Booking Refundable type will be retur ned in 
the response.

o In Language guest level attributes such as first na me, last name 
and middle name will be returned in the response un der “LNG” 
contact type. This information will be captured and  
maintainded for Chinese markets.

can be requested by setting the group identificatio n number and 
the evaluation flags. Transfer eligibility and the reason code 
will be returned in the response. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

33.5.3 Use Case  
33.5.3.1  Sample Message Request  
John has a reservation with id 8308 currently in of fered status for a cruise on one of the 
Royal Caribbean International's ships.  John wants to be sure his cruise details are 
accurately captured by his agent and they retrieve the booking. 
 
<m:retrieveBooking  xmlns:m =" http://services.rccl.com/Interfaces/RetrieveBooking ">  
  <m0:OTA_ReadRQ  MaxResponses =" 030 " MoreDataEchoToken =" 01 " MoreIndicator =" false " 
RetransmissionIndicator =" false " SequenceNmbr =" 1" Target =" Test " TimeStamp =" 2008-05-16T13:51:14 " 
TransactionStatusCode =" Start " Version =" 2.0 ">  
    <m0:POS > 
   … 
    </ m0:POS > 
    <m0:UniqueID  ID =" 8308 " Type =" 14 "/>

</ m:retrieveBooking >

accurately captured by his agent and pricing matche s with the Confirmation document 
that he has received.

Page 262 of 382 34. Get Booking List Message 
34.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Get Booking List message is used to retrieve a list of bookings matching the 
search filter provided in the request. 
34.2 Transaction Services 
• This transaction only returns bookings belonging to  the agency specified in 
the POS message header. 
 
• The message will return a maximum of 20 bookings pe r response. 
 
• The partner will be able to use the following optio nal search filters: 
 
/square4 Sail date 
/square4 Ship code 
/square4 Brand 
/square4 Guest last name 
/square4 Passenger Identification Number 
/square4 Consumer Id 
/square4 Booking Type (FIT or Groups) 
 
• Individual Bookings to Groups Transfer :  
 
Individual Bookings into Group Reservation transfer  eligibility can be 
requested by setting the group identification numbe r and the evaluation flags. 
Booking list response would indicate the transfer e ligibility for all bookings 
returned. In addition, an indicator can be set in t he request to exclude all 
transfer ineligible bookings based on the group id set. 
 
/square4 Booking into Groups Evaluation Requested Flag 
/square4 Exclude transfer ineligible bookings 
 
• Even though these are optional filters, the more th e partner provides, the better 
results the message will return.  Therefore, provid e as many data parameters 
as possible. 
 
• The guest last name is not used as a discrete searc h filter – it will not match 
the exact last name provided.  The serch filter is actually used as a position 
cursor.  Therefore, the response will include the n ext 20 matching bookings 
starting with the booking whose primary passenger’s  last name is 
alphabetically after the provided guest last name s earch filter. 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 263 of 382 • The message supports paging via MaxResponses and Mo reDataEchoToken. 
 
34.3 Typical Process Flows 
 
 
 
34.4 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Retrieve Booking request and respon se are OTA_ReadRQ and 
OTA_ResRetrieveRS.  Our implementation is based on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.

/square4 Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information

required.

• Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
• ReservationInfo/ReservationID is intended to be use d for RCL Reservation ID 
only.  PNRs are not supported. 
• Air, Hotel, Golf and Vehicle reservation elements a re commented out and the 
values for those will not be provided in the respon se.

Page 269 of 382 35. Release Booking Message 
35.1 Functional Overview 
 
The Release Booking message uses the RCL booking ID  to release the lock on the 
booking so that it can be modified by another agent  or program. 
The same message can be used to release bookings un der group reservations as well. 
35.2 Transaction Services 
• This transaction releases the lock on the booking s o that other clients can 
retrieve or update the booking. 
 
35.3 Typical Process Flows 
 
 
 
35.4 Schema Specification 
The schemas for Retrieve Booking request and respon se are OTA_ReadRQ and 
OTA_ResRetrieveRS.  Our implementation is based on the OTA_2007A schema 
specification.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

/square4 Please review the overall constraints and restricti ons section for additional 
information 
/square4 Only the CruiseReadRequest and ReadRequest elements  are supported and 
required. 
/square4 Only one occurrence of ReservationID is supported.

ISOCurrency =" USD ">

        </ BookingChannel > 
      </ Source > 
    </ POS >

      </ CruiseReadRequest > 
    </ ReadRequests > 
  </ OTA_ReadRQ > 
</ m:releaseBooking >

Page 272 of 382  
36. Cruise Booking History Message 
36.1 Functional Overview 
This common transaction uses the booking ID (or) Gr oup ID (or) Group ID and 
Group booking ID assigned by RCL to get the audit t rail history related to that 
booking or a Group.  
The Cruise Booking History message requests change/ service history on an existing 
reservation (Individual reservation, Group Reservat ion or Group Booking 
Reservation). The request message is the OTA_ReadRQ  where the user can specify 
the Reservation ID for which one wishes to see the change history. The response 
message OTA_CruiseBookingHistoryRS returns a list o f history entries for the 
reservation changes that have taken place. 
 
The Boolean MoreDataIndicator attribute in the resp onse will indicate the existence 
of more records that can be retrieved from the rese rvation system. If more data is 
available, then the MoreDataEchoToken attribute in the response will return the 
identifier for the last record returned in the curr ent response.  The data is returned 
back in chronological order. 
36.1.1 Transaction Services 
• Provides paging capability. The attributes MoreData EchoToken and 
MaxResponse ( up to a maximum of 120) under Respons eGroup are used in 
order to pass the values pertaining to the page dow n capability. The request 
should put the maximum history records that it want s returned as a part of the 
response under MaxResponses.  
• When requesting for Group or Group booking service history, the audit trail 
returned will be specific to the requestor (Group S hell owner vs Group 
Booking owner). 
36.2 Typical Process Flow 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

/ OTA_CruiseBookingHistoryRS

39. PromoSearchBreakDown Message 
39.1 Functional Overview 
 
This transaction returns detailed Occupancy and Gue st Level pricing break down for a 
given category and promotional fare. Additionally i t returns few promotional attibutes in 
the response. 
 
This service is mainly introduced to complement the  Category List result set. Categoy 
pricing returns only the consolidated promotion amo unt, concatenated list of promotion 
class and Types for categories/PriceInfo combinatio n. This new service will return the Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 286 of 382 detailed breakdown of promotions that contributed t owards the 
BESTRATE/BVL/Combinable promotional pricing calcula tion. 
The Service validates all input qualifiers and goes  through all pricing and promotions 
eligibility rules and calculation. 
39.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• All Guest level promotional qualifiers should be en tered. 
 
• All pricing rules applied in category list message is applied here as well. 
  
• BESTRATE/BVL pricing can be requested by setting al l the eligible qualifiers in 
the request. 
 
• Service capability is extended to group bookings as  well. 
 
• Optional filter can be set to Exclude Non-Refundabl e promotions when requesting 
for Bestrate, Best Value or any selected promotions . 
 
39.2 Typical Process Flow 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

DetailedPromotions/PricingBreakDown PromoSearchBreakDown CategoryList

Please refer error code appendix for a list of OTA error codes.   Note – At this time, OTA 
is yet to provide a numbering scheme for Cruise err or codes. 
39.6 Special Design Considerations 
• Status code in FareCodeOption element is an OTA_Cod eType (Code List 
Name = Status). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix for  more information. 
• Discount types in FareCodeOption element is an OTA_ CodeType (Code List 
Name = Discount_Type). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appen dix for more 
information. 
• Promotion Class in FareCodeOption element is an OTA _CodeType (Code 
List Name = Promotion_Class). Refer to OTA_CodeType s appendix for more 
information. 
• Promotion Type in FareCodeOption element is an OTA_ CodeType (Code List 
Name = Promotion_Type). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appe ndix for more 
information. 
• ValueAddType in FareCodeOption element is an OTA_Co deType (Code List 
Name = Offer_Type). Refer to OTA_CodeTypes appendix  for more 
information. 
 
40. PromoDetailBreakDown Message 
40.1 Functional Overview 
 Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 294 of 382 This transaction returns the description, expiratio n date, rules, restrictions and other 
associated details of a selected promotional fare(s ) in free form text format. This is an 
enhanced version of Cruise Fare Detail Message. 
40.1.1 Transaction Services 
 
• Returns all details pertaining to a fare code(s) in cluding restrictions and fare rules. 
Fare Detail will be returned for upto 10 fare codes  in the request. 
 
40.2 Typical Process Flow 
RCCL Partner 
getPromoDetailBreakDown 
/ OTA_CruiseFareAvailRQ 
/ OTA_CruiseFareAvailRS 
Available Fares Fare ListSailing List
Package List
/ OTA_CruiseFareAvailRQ 
PromoDetailBreakDown 
Fare Detail Info / OTA_CruiseFareAvailRS 
 
 
40.3 Schema Specification 
The schemas for PromoDetailBreakDown request and re sponse are 
OTA_CruiseFareAvailRQ and OTA_CruiseFareAvailRS.  O ur implementation is based 
on the OTA_2007A schema specification.  Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

Point of Sale (POS) 
 
<xs:complexType name="POS_Type"> 
      <xs:annotation> 
         <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">Point of S ale (POS) is the details identifying the party or c onnection 
channel making the request.</xs:documentation> 
      </xs:annotation> 
      <xs:sequence>

            <xs:annotation> 
               <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">This  holds details regarding the requestor. It may be r epeated to also 
accommodate the delivery systems.</xs:documentation > 
            </xs:annotation> 
         </xs:element> 
      </xs:sequence> 
</xs:complexType>  
   
Errors 
 
   <xs:complexType name="ErrorType"> 
      <xs:annotation> 
         <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">Standard w ay to indicate that an error occurred during the pr ocessing of 
an OTA message</xs:documentation> 
      </xs:annotation> 
      <xs:simpleContent> 
         <xs:extension base="FreeTextType"> 
            <xs:attribute name="Type" type="OTA_Cod eType" use="required"> 
               <xs:annotation> 
                  <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">T he Error element MUST contain the Type attribute th at uses a 
recommended set of values to indicate the error typ e. The validating XSD can expect to accept values t hat it has 
NOT been explicitly coded for and process them by u sing Type ="Unknown".  Refer to OTA Code List Error  
Warning Type (EWT).</xs:documentation> 
               </xs:annotation> 
            </xs:attribute> 
            <xs:attributeGroup ref="ErrorWarningAtt ributeGroup"/> 
            <xs:attribute name="NodeList" type="xs: string"> 
               <xs:annotation> 
                  <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">A n XPath expression that selects all the nodes whose  data caused 
this error.  Further, this expression should have a n    additional contraint which contains the data o f the node.  This 
will provide the offending data back to systems tha t cannot maintain the original message. </xs:docume ntation> 
               </xs:annotation> 
            </xs:attribute> 
         </xs:extension> 
      </xs:simpleContent> 
   </xs:complexType> 
   <xs:complexType name="ErrorsType"> 
      <xs:annotation> Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary 
 
Page 300 of 382          <xs:documentation xml:lang="en">A collecti on of errors that occurred during the processing of  a 
message.</xs:documentation>

Code  Description  
2LWR 2 lower twin beds 
3LWR 3 lower twin beds 
4LWR 4 lower twin beds may convert to 1 or 2 queens  
CONV 2 lower twin beds may convert to queen 
CRIB Cribs 
DBED Double Bed 
HDCP Handicap - details are in cabin description 
KING 2 lower full beds may convert to king 
QBED Queen Size Bed 
ROLL Rollaway Bed 
UPLW 1 lower bed and 1 pullman upper Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

Page 381 of 382 APPENDIX F – Communication and Connectivity 
 
This section depicts the communication and connecti vity mechanism that needs to be 
employed in order to invoke all the API transaction s that are mentioned in this document. 
 
As depicted below, all communication to the RCL res ervation system using the APIs 
needs to be conducted using web service calls by th e RCL partners. These web service 
call invocations should be considered stateless and  the underlying protocol that will be 
used for all communication will be secure HTTP (HTT PS). 
 
 
 
 
More detailed content for this section will be prov ided in the next RCL API 
specifications release. Royal Caribbean Cruises, Ltd.  Confidential and Pro prietary

The content for this section is partner environment  specific and will be provided 
separately to each partner.
